Economic Supplement

Reading the National General Budget for the 25th Year 200

— Wei Youfei

The general outline of the budget for the 25th year was compiled by the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics in mid-May and passed by the Central Political Council in mid-June. Subsequently, the Executive Yuan, based on the general outline, compiled the general budget, which was passed by the Legislative Yuan on June 30th and officially promulgated. This time, the budget figure was reduced by approximately 20 million yuan compared to the draft general outline prepared by the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics. According to the official document submitted by the Executive Yuan to the Legislative Yuan, the originally planned revenue and expenditure exceeded 1 billion yuan. While the revenue and expenditure appeared balanced on the surface, the revenue portion, as proposed by the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics, included an additional 180 million yuan in debt income, 10 million yuan in net profit from state-owned businesses, and 12 million yuan in consolidated taxes, resulting in an actual difference of over 20 million yuan. In order to achieve a balanced revenue and expenditure and consolidate the credit of the legal tender, the review was based on the following three principles: (1) Regular expenses should not exceed the approved budget amount from the previous year; (2) Newly established agencies should be postponed if not necessary; (3) Temporary expenses should not be included if not necessary. These three principles were used to reduce expenditures, resulting in a total amount of 990,658,450 yuan.

According to the budget for the 25th year published by the Legislative Yuan this time, the total amount is slightly inflated compared to the 24th year, with an increase of 30 million yuan. The detailed items of various revenues and expenditures have both increases and decreases. The items with larger increases and decreases are as follows: (Unit: 1,000 yuan)

Under Revenue Items

Consolidated Tax Increase 18,254

Debt Increase 55,000

Customs Duties Decrease 23,424

Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Decrease 4,781

State-Owned Revenue Decrease 3,067

Other Decrease 13,588

Under Expenditure Items

State Affairs Expenses Increase 2,410

Internal Affairs Expenses Increase 4,232

Education and Culture Expenses Increase 6,836

Construction Expenses Increase 16,719

State-Owned Business Capital Increase 53,367

Party Affairs Expenses Decrease 2,452

Financial Affairs Expenses Decrease 5,911

Debt Expenses Decrease 35,765

Among the above-listed increases and decreases, this year's budget is an improvement over previous years. This is because government affairs expenses are generally slightly reduced compared to last year. Even party affairs expenses, which have been expanding year by year since the 21st year of the Republic, have been reduced this year. At the same time, education and culture expenses and construction expenses have all increased slightly. From the perspective of the general public, the reduction in consumptive expenditures in the allocation of expenditures is beneficial.

However, upon careful analysis of the various figures, this year's budget still cannot escape the established patterns of previous years' budgets. In terms of revenue, customs duties still occupy the first place in terms of figures. Furthermore, the total amount of the six indirect tax items, including salt tax, tobacco and alcohol tax, stamp tax, consolidated tax, and mining tax, reaches more than 650 million yuan, accounting for 67% of the total revenue. The next most important source of revenue is debt income, accounting for about 13% of the total. The next most important source of revenue is the three direct tax items, namely the exchange tax, transaction tax, income tax, and bank tax, accounting for 8% of the total revenue. The remaining 2% is other income. Therefore, indirect taxes and debt income still occupy an important position of 80% in the total revenue, while direct taxes are only secondary.

In terms of expenditure, military expenses still rank first, debt expenses still rank second, and the ratio between the total amount of various consumptive expenditures and non-consumptive expenditures is still very large. Therefore, whether viewed from the perspective of revenue or expenditure, this year's national general budget has made progress in terms of principles. However, strictly speaking in terms of actual revenue and expenditure, the improvements are still very few.

The Executive Yuan reduced the total revenue and expenditure figures of the general outline by 20 million yuan, mostly due to the reduction in actual revenue. In order to strive for a balanced revenue and expenditure in reality, the figures for revenue were reduced on the one hand, and the figures for expenditure were reduced on the other hand, which shows the seriousness of the published budget this time. The Executive Yuan has already considered the expenditure aspect, and further reductions are of course impossible. Therefore, let us discuss the revenue figures here.

A tax system centered on indirect taxes is not only highly flexible but also absolutely harmful to the national economy, and the distribution is unfair, which is not in line with general tax principles. This has already been a consensus among the government and the public. However, this year's budget still cannot break away from the indirect tax-centered system. Of course, fiscal reform may not be consistent in theory and practice and cannot be achieved overnight. What is worrisome is that there may already be problems with the various indirect tax items in this year's budget as listed in the budget. Under the customs duty item, due to the decline in national purchasing power and the decline in import and export trade in recent years, it has been gradually decreasing. The increasingly serious problem of smuggling in North China in the past six months has also created a huge obstacle to customs revenue. The Executive Yuan also considered this point in its official document to the Legislative Yuan, but only added a caveat of strictly cracking down on smuggling. Although the customs duty figure in this budget has been reduced by more than 20 million yuan, according to the customs statistics last year, customs revenue has already decreased by 20 million yuan compared to previous years. In the first quarter of this year, the customs revenue in North China mostly decreased by more than 28%. Therefore, even if smuggling is strictly cracked down on as soon as possible, I am afraid that the amount of the decrease will definitely be more than 20 million yuan.

Here, let's first mention the consolidated tax, which ranks third among the indirect taxes. According to the national budget in recent years, the position of the consolidated tax in revenue has been gradually increasing. In fact, the actual amount collected each year is also more than the budget. In recent years, the decrease in customs revenue has been compensated for by the consolidated tax, which is not a bad method. However, the increased burden of the consolidated tax on the national production industry is certainly debatable, and in recent years, the national industries that can be called national industries are almost all struggling in hardship. Therefore, while methods can certainly be used to increase the income of the consolidated tax, in fact, it is feared that the consolidated tax will also decrease due to the dimness of various industries. What is even more worrisome is that in today's world of rampant smuggled goods, the resistance of national industries in the market is gradually weakening, and the income of the consolidated tax will definitely feel reduced. From the perspective of the budget itself, whether the actual amount collected of the consolidated tax at the end of this year will exceed the budget as in previous years is another debatable point.

The second largest indirect tax is the salt tax. The increase in the salt tax affects the common people, and its harm is greater than that of the consolidated tax. The actual amount of salt tax collected each year has also been increasing year by year, according to recent budgets. However, the reason for the increase is not natural but artificial. In many salt-producing areas, there is a trend of increasing production, creating a situation of hoarding salt, which is close to prepaid. At the same time, some salt-producing areas have gradually become integrated with the problem of smuggling and tax evasion, which will also be a national problem in terms of actual collection in the future.

The three items under direct taxes, such as the exchange tax, have been included in the budget for more than a year. According to the recent announcement by the government of the draft treaty on inheritance tax and income tax, it may be possible to see the realization of the attempt to replace indirect taxes with direct taxes in the future. However, according to the figures in this year's budget, the figures for these direct taxes have not been expanded compared to previous years, which shows that the implementation period must still be awaited.

According to general fiscal principles, recurring revenue should be listed as recurring expenditure, and temporary revenue should be listed as temporary expenditure. Therefore, all debt income should be treated as temporary revenue. Although debt income is included in the temporary sector in this national general budget, there is already a slight imbalance between the total amount of recurring revenue and expenditure. If the budgets of previous years are examined, a principle can be obtained: that is, no matter what position tax revenue occupies in the total revenue of each year's budget, if the percentage of tax revenue and the percentage of debt income are added together, the number is the same. In other words, if tax revenue increases in a certain year, debt income decreases; if tax revenue decreases, borrowing increases. Therefore, using debt income to cover budget deficits has become a common occurrence. On the surface, debt income is in the temporary revenue sector, but in reality, it has long been allocated for recurring purposes. If indirect taxes are reduced this year and direct taxes have not yet started, according to past practice, this difference can be added to the debt. However, since the issuance of the National Unification and Reconstruction Bonds in February, this huge figure has been unprecedented. In terms of the limit of market purchases, the possibility of re-issuing new bonds is extremely small. Even the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics of the National Government believes that regarding future borrowing: "The government is currently using the method of consolidating public debt to complete the legal tender policy and balance national treasury revenue and expenditure, which is a suitable policy for dealing with times of national crisis. However, the current subscribers to this public debt are mainly banks, and the power to purchase public debt is limited to the amount of new deposits added by banks. If public debt is issued beyond this limit, it will inevitably lead to inflation." Since our country's financial organization is not completely consolidated and the public lacks knowledge of currency, inflation will naturally be harmful to the national economy.

If attention is paid to the expenditure of debt expenses at the same time as the debt income item, there is another point worth noting. That is, the expenditure of debt expenses is almost equal to half of the debt income. Therefore, using the method of borrowing to make up for the budget deficit, even if there is no problem with the issuance, the increase in debt expenses is tantamount to preparing for the increase in the deficit in the second year, which is a prepaid nature. According to the current reduced debt expenses, it already occupies a very important position in finance, let alone increasing it further? Therefore, using debt income to cover the deficit is definitely not a solution.

The Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics of the National Government put forward six suggestions for making up for the budget balance, namely: (1) The operating surplus of the Central Bank is not yet included in the budget; (2) The unified public debt is from the salt of Lu, and about 180 million yuan of face value can be left; (3) The increase in the consolidated tax; (4) The levying of direct taxes; (5) There are domestic and foreign debt reserves in the debt expenses that can be transferred; (6) The debt expenses have a slight surplus. Some of the above six suggestions can only be regarded as special circumstances, because they are definitely not something that can be had every year. Even if this year's budget can be made up for by using the above six methods, the balance of revenue and expenditure in the future is still a problem.

According to one of the principles of the Executive Yuan's budget reduction, temporary expenses should not be included if they are not necessary, which shows that there is still a great range of flexibility left in the expenditure aspect.

In short, after reading this year's general budget, it is very clear that considerable efforts are still needed to achieve a balanced revenue and expenditure. The main reason why it is difficult to balance revenue and expenditure is that there can be no thorough improvement in revenue and expenditure. Therefore, in addition to throttling spending, the maintenance of indirect tax revenue requires strict anti-smuggling methods to prevent the intrusion of smuggling, while moving direct taxes from paper to implementation is even more urgent. This is still peacetime finance. If it comes to a non-ordinary period, the question of budget balance and the threat of deficits will of course be greater than it is now, which is even more necessary to prepare for in advance. (July 2nd)

A Study of Federal Reserve Credit Dynamics 201

— Liu Kongjun

The changes in the outstanding amount of the U.S. Federal Reserve Bank Credit can be observed through its weekly periodic reports, which indicate the factors that increase or decrease the outstanding amount of the Federal Reserve Bank. The numbers listed in the report for the week of January 9, 1935, are reprinted as follows:

Table of Factors Increasing or Decreasing Outstanding Federal Reserve Bank Credit (Unit: Millions of U.S. Dollars (+) Increase (-) Decrease)

| | 1935 | 1934 |

|----------------|-------------|-------------|

| | January 9 | January 2 | January 10 |

| Discounted Notes | 7 | ... | (-)97 |

| Purchased Notes | 6 | ... | (-)109 |

| U.S. Government Securities | 2,430 | (-)1 | (-)2 |

| Industrial Advances (Note) | 15 | (+)1 | (+)15 |

| Other Reserve Bank Credit | 9 | (+)6 | (+)1 |

| Total Reserve Bank Credit | 2,467 | (+)6 | (-)188 |

| Gold Coin and Currency in Stock | 8,258 | (+)15 | (+)4,222 |

| Treasury and National Bank Currency | 2,508 | (-)6 | (+)206 |

| Currency in Circulation | 5,420 | (-)24 | (+)23 |

| Member Bank Reserve Balances | 4,283 | (+)193 | (+)1,506 |

| Treasury Cash and Deposits in Federal Reserve Banks | 3,094 | (-)70 | (+)2,741 |

| Non-Member Deposits and Other Federal Reserve Items | 436 | (+)6 | (-)31 |

(Note) Does not include $10,000,000 in entrusted funds

The above report is now explained item by item to understand the importance of Federal Reserve credit:

(1) Discounted Notes: This item represents loans from member banks to the Reserve Bank, which are used to supplement reserve balances. There are various factors for the increase in loans, such as (A) an increase in member bank deposits; (B) the Reserve Bank selling securities or accepting notes; (C) gold exports or designated uses; (D) an increase in currency in circulation; and (E) an increase in non-member bank deposits in the Reserve Bank. Other items in the report are also helpful in explaining the reasons for the increase or decrease in member bank borrowing from the Reserve Bank.

(2) Purchased Notes and U.S. Government Securities: These two items reflect the Reserve Bank's operations in the public market. An increase in holdings of accepted notes or government securities places federal funds at the disposal of member banks; conversely, a decrease reduces the amount of Federal Reserve credit. Changes in these two items can indicate the public market policy adopted by the Reserve System. An increase in public market purchases indicates the Reserve Bank's aim to stabilize the financial market.

(3) Industrial Advances: This item includes loans to private enterprises made in accordance with the regulations of June 19, 1934. In terms of the relationship with the financial market, this type of lending is no different from discounted notes.

(4) Other Reserve Bank Credit: This item represents several detailed items, such as so-called "Float," which occurs in the Reserve Bank System as an agent for commercial banks to collect checks and drafts. "Float" is different from "Uncollected Items" and "Deferred Availability Items." In other words, it is the credit given by the Reserve Bank to commercial banks that the commercial banks have not yet received. This item also includes bonds of the Federal Intermediate Credit Bank, bonds of the Federal Land Bank, municipal bonds, and debts owed by foreign central banks held by the Reserve Bank.

(5) Total Reserve Bank Credit: This is the sum of the above five items and is the total outstanding amount of Federal Reserve Bank credit.

(6) Gold Coin and Currency in Stock: This item represents the total amount of gold held by the Treasury. An increase in gold, whether due to imports, exemption from designated uses, or new production, is sufficient to increase member bank reserve balances. This is because gold must be sold to the Treasury or the Reserve Bank, and the check paid for it is deposited into the member bank's account at the Reserve Bank.

(7) Treasury and National Bank Currency: This item represents the currency issued by the Treasury to supplement the financial system and directly bears its responsibility. An increase in this item is a symbol of the Treasury's issuance of large amounts of currency, which results in an increase in the balance of member banks' deposits at the Reserve Bank.

(8) Currency in Circulation: This item represents the total amount of various actual circulating currencies. A decrease in the amount of currency in circulation reduces the amount of member bank reserve balances because currency is obtained by member banks from the Reserve Bank, and their repayment of banknotes is taken from their reserve balances. Conversely, a decrease in the amount of currency results in an increase in member bank balances because member banks return unneeded currency to the Reserve Bank.

(9) Treasury Cash and Deposits in Federal Reserve Banks: This item represents the funds available to the Treasury, which is different from the funds deposited by the Treasury in commercial banks from the sale of government securities. It includes gold, exchange stabilization funds, general funds, and currency held by the Treasury, as well as government deposits in the Reserve Bank. A decrease in this item is sufficient to indicate that the Treasury has transferred cash or Reserve Bank deposits to the banking sector, resulting in an increase in member bank reserve balances. An increase in this item can indicate that cash has been paid into the Treasury, or that the Treasury has transferred deposits from commercial banks to the Reserve Bank, and the reserve balances of member banks decrease accordingly.

(10) Non-Member Bank Deposits and Other Federal Reserve Items: This item includes a number of detailed items, with non-member bank deposits being the most important. Non-member banks maintain deposits in the Reserve Bank for clearing purposes. A decrease in this balance results in an increase in member bank reserve balances because the funds lost by non-member banks are transferred to member banks.

Based on the above simple explanation, it can be determined what factors should be responsible for the $193.3 million decrease in member bank reserve balances in the weekly report of January 9, 1935.

Factors Increasing Member Bank Reserve Balances

1. Increase in Industrial Advances 1,000,000

2. Increase in Other Reserve Bank Credit 6,000,000

3. Increase in Gold Coin and Currency in Stock 15,000,000

4. Decrease in Currency in Circulation 114,000,000

5. Decrease in Treasury Cash and Deposits in Federal Reserve Banks 70,000,000

Total Increase 206,000,000

Factors Decreasing Member Bank Reserve Balances

1. Decrease in U.S. Treasury Securities 1,000,000

2. Decrease in Treasury and National Bank Currency 6,000,000

3. Increase in Non-Member Bank Deposits and Other Federal Reserve Items 6,000,000

Total Decrease 13,000,000

Total Increase in Member Bank Reserve Balances 193,000,000

In recent years, the development of finance and the promulgation of new banking and monetary laws during the Roosevelt administration have brought about tremendous changes in the power of the Federal Reserve System to manage credit. Under the control of the new laws, the old tools for managing credit no longer exist. The Reserve Bank no longer uses the discount rate and public market operations as the basis for manipulating bank credit. Instead, there are new forces at play.

Since the outbreak of the commercial depression in 1929, member banks began to increase their reserve balances above the legal limit. This effect was partly due to the contraction of bank credit, partly due to the inflow of gold, and partly due to the Reserve Bank's adoption of a sound monetary policy. In 1932, the Reserve Bank began to jointly purchase large amounts of government securities. Within a few months, its holdings increased by $1.1 billion. The aim of this policy was to increase the excess reserves of member banks in order to curb the contraction of credit and encourage its expansion. Although the result was not effective, this policy was implemented again in 1933. At this time, the Reserve Bank further increased its holdings of government securities by more than $600 million. The only effect of this was to increase the reserve balances of member banks to an unprecedented proportion. In September 1934, excess reserves reached as much as $2 billion.

Under these circumstances, the discount rate of the Reserve Bank became insignificant. Member banks reduced their borrowing from the Reserve Bank to a negligible amount, so that in theory, although their loans and deposits expanded by $20 billion, the credit of the Reserve Bank did not expand accordingly. The Reserve Bank holds approximately $2.43 billion in government securities, which could be sold in the public market to eliminate the excess reserves of member banks. However, this plan would have a huge impact on the government securities market by lowering market prices. Given the Treasury's heavy responsibility to assist the government in implementing its recovery plan, it is self-evident that it would not adopt such a plan.

In fact, the power to manage member bank reserve balances today has largely shifted to the Treasury. This development is mostly due to the devaluation of the U.S. dollar and the revaluation of domestic gold coin and currency, which gave the Treasury a profit of $2.8 billion. Of this, $2 billion was allocated to the stabilization fund, and the remainder was added to the general fund for gold. However, in terms of credit, the distinction is irrelevant. The important point is that the Treasury's consumption of gold, other than exporting gold, will have the same increase in member bank reserve balances.

The Treasury can use a portion of the gold to meet the country's liquid expenditures. The method is to deposit gold certificates in the Reserve Bank. This action increases the Treasury's deposits at the Reserve Bank, which is used to issue checks to repay debts. The checks issued are deposited in commercial banks, and finally returned to the Reserve Bank for payment. The Reserve Bank then often credits the member bank's account, so the increase in member bank reserve balances is the same as the inflow of gold. On September 19, 1934, the Treasury had more than $3 billion in free gold and deposits in the Reserve Bank. If this amount were spent in its entirety, excess reserves would increase from the current level of $2 billion to $5 billion. Although this development is far from reality, the position of member bank reserves is not so much controlled by the Federal Reserve Bank as it is completely controlled by the Treasury. In fact, because of the stability of the U.S. dollar, the Reserve Bank has only become a tool for the Treasury to increase member bank reserve balances.

A Congressional law stipulates that the total amount of silver purchased at home and abroad should be 25% of the gold currency in stock. This is another reason why the Treasury can increase member bank reserve balances. Since the silver is obtained by the Treasury, the Treasury has the right to issue silver certificates, and the amount of currency is increased accordingly. The increase in currency is not actually necessary, so it returns to the banks, and the banks deposit it in the Reserve Bank, increasing the balance of member banks' deposits in the Reserve Bank. With this effect, the Treasury can interfere with the ordinary actions of the Reserve Bank.

The Treasury's influence on the financial market is so great. However, the Reserve Bank is not unable to manage the expansion of member bank credit. First, according to the Banking Act of 1933 and the Securities Exchange Act, the Reserve Bank has broad powers to regulate mortgage lending, which can curb the expansion of securities lending and prevent speculative frenzies, such as the story of 1928 to 1929. Second, and more importantly, the Agricultural Adjustment Act of May 12, 1933, authorized the Federal Reserve Board, with the approval of the President, to declare an emergency period due to credit expansion. During this period, it can arbitrarily increase or decrease the reserve balances for legally required demand or time deposits at any time. This power is a way for the Federal Reserve Board to eliminate the excess reserves of member banks and restore its ability to manage the current financial market.

However, what should also be studied is that the actions of the Federal Reserve Board in the past to curb credit expansion have often been opposed by the political and business communities. This was the case in both 1920 and 1929. Now, under the guidance of the Treasury, its power has greatly increased compared to before. The Federal Reserve Board has great power to curb credit expansion; its exercise must have the approval and assistance of the government, so the future of the Reserve Bank's management of credit has become a political issue.

In addition to influencing Federal Reserve policy and using free gold and issuing silver certificates to affect member bank reserve balances, the Treasury can also use ordinary financial resources to influence the financial market under normal circumstances. On the 15th of March, June, September, and December of each year, the Treasury engages in collecting taxes, recovering funds, and using bank funds to pay interest on government debt, selling Treasury bills, debt certificates, long-term bonds, and repaying matured issues. Although the amount of transactions is huge, the Treasury's advanced investment techniques ensure that the financial market does not experience any disturbances, and interest rates are not subject to temporary fluctuations.

The details and amounts of this technical defense investment vary from time to time, and the factors that govern it are various, such as the Treasury's cash balance, the government's financial needs for the next quarter, the budgeted amount of tax collection, the situation in the government securities market, and the amount of debt repayment due. The Treasury's seasonal financial operations begin on the 15th, releasing funds to pay interest on public debt, repay short-term Treasury bills, and for special purposes—such as the old-age military officer loans on March 15, 1931—payment is made with checks from the Reserve Bank, and the recipients deposit them in commercial banks, which in turn deposit them in the Reserve Bank. The result is an increase in member bank reserve balances. At the same time, the Treasury receives checks from commercial banks, which are used to pay taxes and the Treasury's new debts. The collection of these checks is debited to member banks' deposits at the Reserve Bank, resulting in the opposite of payment.

If the payments and receipts match, member bank reserve balances will not change. However, in practice, receipts often lag payments by several days, and the Treasury relies on borrowing from the Reserve Bank as the only way to settle its debts during this period. The borrowing method is to adopt debt certificates with a special date, the amount of which can be as high as hundreds of millions of dollars, which are rolled over daily and reduced according to the amount of income.

This borrowing is credited to the Treasury's account at the Reserve Bank for the Treasury's use, which results in the expansion of Federal Reserve Bank credit and increases member bank deposits. Under normal circumstances, this can provide temporary artificial stability to the market. There are several ways to prevent this situation from occurring: First, the Reserve Bank sells the special Treasury debt certificates it participates in to member banks (mostly in New York), and spends the funds under the reserve balance. Second, the Reserve Bank sells government securities in the public market or reduces its holdings of accepted bills, and all maturing bills are not replenished, so that the impact of the Treasury's borrowing can be offset. However, this method is not easy to implement. For example, in 1934, the Reserve Bank's sale of a small amount of savings had an adverse impact on the market price of government securities, which would contradict the government's fiscal policy. At the same time, the holdings of accepted bills are extremely small, and the non-replenishment of maturing bills is not enough to affect the reserve balances of member banks. Finally (the third method), the New York Reserve Bank is allowed to temporarily fall below the legal limit, so that the lack before the Treasury's operation is corrected by excess reserves a few days later.

Although most of the Treasury's operations are concentrated in the tax collection season and the interest payment period, its constant dealings with the banking sector have a greater impact on the credit situation than seasonal investment. According to convention, the Treasury keeps a large amount of cash and deposits it in domestic commercial banks, and the checks it issues are drawn on its deposits at the Reserve Bank. Only when necessary will the deposits in commercial banks be transferred to the Reserve Bank.

Therefore, the Treasury's routine operations cause funds to move between the Reserve Bank and commercial banks in two ways: On the one hand, the Treasury draws checks on its deposits at the Reserve Bank, which are deposited in member banks, and finally credited to the Reserve Bank's account again; on the other hand, the Treasury withdraws deposits from commercial banks and deposits them in the Reserve Bank, which results in expenditures from the Reserve Bank's member account. Therefore, unless the amounts of receipts and payments are the same, the reserve balances of member banks will be affected. For example, at the end of the week of September 26, 1934, member bank reserves increased by $81 million, mostly due to the $63 million decrease in the Treasury's cash and deposits in the Federal Reserve Bank.

Commercial News

Securities: Big Players Continuously Buying, Government Bonds Steadily Rose Last Week 202

Increased by $1.89 to $2.65. Afternoon Trading Temporarily Suspended for Three Weeks Starting Today.

Last week, from July 6th to 11th, the market situation on the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange gradually rose and was quite tight. It was the first good market since the Guangdong-Guangxi Incident. It was more than $3 higher than the lowest price. Compared to the highest price, with Type A bonds, it was only more than $1 lower. The situation in Guangdong and Guangxi became increasingly chaotic due to internal strife. General short-covering and large players going long at the same time caused the market to rebound and rise sharply. However, there are still problems with the Guangdong affair, and the North China Incident is becoming more and more difficult. Although various parties are single-mindedly moving forward, future changes will still involve fierce ups and downs. Reviewing last week, on Monday, there were rumors in the market about Fujian, down by 5.7 cents, and the trend was for three consecutive small declines. The market rebounded at the close. On Tuesday, the situation was depressing, brewing for change. On the 4th, buying resumed, and the market immediately rebounded by half a dollar. On Wednesday, retail investors covered shorts, and large players also bought in, causing a strong rebound and a sharp rise of about $1. On Thursday, the appetite of large players became stronger, and retail investors covered even more enthusiastically, causing a large rise of 78 cents to $1.45. The market price in August repeatedly reached new highs. On Friday, some bulls exited, causing a slight decline of 23 cents, but the trend remained firm. On Saturday, large players continued to buy in, and there were also certain rumors in the market, causing the market price to rebound again, rising by several cents to more than $1. The high market prices in recent days, although due to changes in the situation and short-covering, were also due to a large number of speculators going long. Therefore, if the long side wavers slightly, the short side will surge, and there will be many more waves in the future. As a result of the week's market prices, all rose by $1.89 to $2.65. The total transaction volume was $52.6 million. In addition, the exchange announced that due to the hot weather, afternoon trading will be temporarily suspended for one week starting today, and will resume as usual on August 1st. Cotton Yarn: Cotton Farmers Hedging, U.S. Cotton Prices Rebounded 203

Yesterday, U.S. cotton opened with prices falling by 6 points and rising by 2 points for various months. The market was active in the morning, but the news from Liverpool was not good. Liverpool and mainland dealers sold, and cotton farmers hedged, and bulls took profits, causing prices to rebound. Afterwards, industry peers, Wall Street, and the Far East bought in, and shorts covered when prices fell, resulting in a slight rebound. Currently, the focus is on the need for rain in the early-growing areas. Borrowed cotton has been sold off in the South. Textiles have been in short supply during the week. The closing price was stable. Spot prices fell by 6 points, and futures fell by 6 to 11 points. English cotton spot prices rose by 8 points, and futures fell by 12 points. Indian cotton initially fell due to large-scale bull profit-taking, but later strengthened due to buying by Japanese merchants, European exporters, and futures traders. Bengal rose by 1.25 to 3.25 rupees, Oomra rose by 1.5 to 3.5 rupees, and Broach rose by 0.75 to 2.75 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (telegram of the 11th):

Tidbits 207

— (Liu Fangdi)

Fire tests gold; adversity tests heroes.

Everything that creates virtue is cruel.

The greatest pain is nothing more than being blamed by one's own conscience.

Young people should cherish their careers as much as they cherish their youth.

Women's faces and warriors' guns equally create a history of humanity.

Integrity is a moral sentiment; piety is a religious sentiment.

Do not accept even a small favor from a mean person, for it will become your lifelong burden.

History is always sacrificing human lives; the new light of history must come from hell.

Although love is as intoxicating as a rose, it is also as thorny as a rose.

Major events always happen by chance. But in a moment of chance, our fate is decided.

Page of Morality 208

— Lanshan

Everyone sighs and says, "Shanghai is a place with poor morals." This is indeed true, but perhaps this is because there are too many people who like to read news about the corruption of morals, so so many events that corrupt morals are happening, right?

When the court hears those scandalous cases—whether it is rape, seduction, or consensual adultery—out of concern for morality, eager onlookers always flock to the court. Young people are particularly curious. When reading the newspaper every day, they first grab the local news section and concentrate on finding records of topics that stimulate their inspiration, chewing them over carefully, the longer the better, with relish.

Middle-aged people are not willing to be left behind. They are also very interested in records of such attractive cases. However, when they read them, they do not show the impetuosity of young people, but pretend to be very stern and cold, so that others do not know that they are reading a piece of news that can make one's heart race and blood surge.

Therefore, we often envy those who are judges. They can sit solemnly in front of the court, facing the man and woman in the case, questioning them about the romantic historical materials of the past, using questions that are as penetrating and all-encompassing as mercury seeping into the ground to press him and her, so that they do not dare to leave out anything and confess truthfully:—When did the relationship start, and where was it?——On such and such a day of such and such a month, another time;—and another encounter. As clear as a running account.——Imagine, what kind of attitude and tone should they have when they describe these sweet and bitter memories shyly? However, we are not judges, so we will never have the opportunity to experience all of this. We can only find the charm in the next day's newspaper and imagine the attitude of the two people at the time.

Since we cannot forget to read these news stories that harm morals, and yet we insist on pretending to be moralists, sighing, "Shanghai is really a place with poor morals!" in order to show our integrity, no wonder the morals of Shanghai are getting worse and worse. I have made such a determination.

Gloves from Caohéjing 209

— Zhu Tingyun

Although Caohéjing is said to be less than ten miles away from the metropolis of Shanghai, it is already a deserted area. Most of the residents make a living by farming. In addition to working in the fields, a group of women weave gloves early and late, so making gloves has become their secondary occupation.

Their tools are very simple. They only need a six-inch-long iron needle. This needle is made of the steel ribs of an umbrella. They thread yarn onto this needle and can weave gloves with various styles of openwork patterns. The styles are very beautiful, such as Dragon Flower Pagoda, Ruyi, pentagonal rhombus, etc. Some even draw the patterns on paper first and then weave them according to the patterns, but this kind of price is relatively more expensive, about eighty cents a pair, and the rest can be bought for fifty or sixty cents a pair. However, when work in the fields is busy, the price will also rise a bit.

As for the name, they do not call them gloves, but hand bags. The sales locations are concentrated in Huangjia Garden and Guanshengyuan, because there are many people who come to play in Shanghai, and they sell them to tourists. It is said that the business is quite satisfactory.

Sea 210

— Gu Guiqiu

My hometown is on the coast of the East China Sea, where there are long embankments and a wide sea.

I remember when I was little, I often hid from my parents and secretly made an appointment with a few little companions to go to the beach to catch crabs, catch mudskippers, catch earthworms... If we caught a lot, we would bring them back for lunch, and the taste was more delicious than anything else.

Driven by life, I left my hometown and left the sea. My hometown has been separated from me for a long time; I have not seen the beauty of my hometown for a long time.

Recently, I went back to my hometown once. In order to find traces of my childhood, I wandered on the beach again. When I was a child, I only felt that the sea was big and wide; but now I have another concept of the sea.

The sea is a vast society. Here, you can sweep away your listlessness and your decadence! It will give you excitement and push you forward! Because the roar of the sea wind represents the roar of the masses; the surging of the sea water symbolizes the revolutionary upsurge!

The sea is a stimulant to me. I want the sea to always be my compass; always be my guiding light!

Don't Be Strained Watching Others Carry Loads 211

The Phoenix Returns to Its Nest 212

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Light Rain and Slanting Wind Still Leave Traces; Quiet Night, Alone Writing a Letter of Severance

After he finished writing, he reread it under the lamp. The letter contained the following passage:

Lan loves novels and literature. This has been the case since childhood, and she is especially impressed by Mr.'s works, which are mournful and beautiful. This can be said frankly and without any need for disguise. However, many people read and admire Mr.'s articles published in newspapers. This private admiration must also be shared by many women in their boudoirs. If Mr. knows this and compares it entirely to Western social interactions between men and women, I think he is very wrong. Who does not admire the poems of the ancients, such as Li Bai and Du Fu, and the prose of Han Yu and Su Shi? If there are women among them, would it be a laughing matter to assume that they admire Li Bai, Du Fu, Han Yu, and Su Shi? My family is a scholarly family. Although women study, they never hear about outside affairs. Mr. relies on his own speculation about the minds of young ladies in their secluded chambers and suddenly sends a letter. This not only shocks and confuses people, but also makes them doubt that someone with Mr.'s literary reputation would do such a thing.

He read this passage to himself four or five times. He held the letter down with both hands and stared at it blankly for a long time. He thought to himself, "These words are heavy enough. A letter of severance is nothing more than this."

Chapter 4: Seeing and Hearing Are Not Always Floating, Doubts Arise and Reappear; Life and Death Can Be Entrusted, Generously Sending Elegies

The emotional impulse of doing things in life always lasts only a short time. The longer the time, the more the emotional turmoil subsides, and then one can realize that what one has done is excessive. Such changes in thought are often found in clear-headed people. Menglan is naturally a smart person. When she received Guoqi's letter, she thought that he would actually go to her relatives' house to investigate, and also write a letter to the school to inquire. This would spread around and more people would know. This not only concerns her own reputation, but also something that her family absolutely cannot tolerate. The consequences of disapproval are hard to say. It is even possible that her life will be in danger. Therefore, based on this starting point, the more she thought about it, the more she felt that the future was terrible. She had to write a letter to cut off Guoqi's path. Therefore, based on her conscious judgment, she wrote several letters in one breath. After she finished writing, she looked at the wording of the letters herself, and it was always too intense. She felt that she had to delete and revise them. However, if she revised them to be more moderate, she would not be able to reject Guoqi's request. This left her sitting quietly under the lamp all night, unable to think of a proper solution. The last letter she wrote was very carefully written, slowly written. But after she finished writing, she spread the letter paper on the table, held her head with both hands, and quietly looked at the two lines of the letter. When she saw the important parts, she would shake her head and could not help but pick up her pen and circle those sentences. After circling them, she continued to look down, and it was still inappropriate, so she had to circle a few more sentences. (Forty-six)

Special Feature

Impressions of the Air Defense and Anti-Poison Knowledge Exhibition (Part 1) 213

— Special

The newspaper has repeatedly revealed that the air defense production exhibition has opened today. The venue is on the second floor of the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao. The reporter drove to visit and met an old classmate who was involved in the preparatory work. He kindly accompanied me to view each section. Now I will write down the impressions I gained from the visit to inform the general public in Shanghai.

A plaque with the words "Air Defense and Anti-Poison Knowledge Exhibition" in white characters on a blue background is hung in front of the door. Turning up the stairs, you can see five airplanes of different sizes, suspended by lead wires, appearing to soar into the sky. There are also items on display on both sides of the entrance to the second floor: On the left, there are two large and small bombs. The small one is a souvenir from the January 28th Shanghai Incident. On the right, there are various anti-poison products from the Civil Chemical Industry Society, including gas masks, anti-poison rubber clothing, boots, hats, etc., all of which we have never seen before. A clay figure wearing anti-poison clothing and a hat stands at the corner of the wall, giving the audience a very profound impression. All the items are produced by the society. Various gas masks from different countries are also displayed on the table for the audience to refer to. One of them was hastily made by various rubber factories when our side feared that the enemy would release poison gas during the January 28th Shanghai Incident. It was very simple and very different from the current gas masks. However, this gas mask has become a historical souvenir and is not easy to obtain, so they feel very precious. The society has specialized personnel to explain the structure and effectiveness of various anti-poison products. Many people gathered around to listen to the lectures and visit. According to the reporter's guess, there are probably not many people who know about various anti-poison products, and there must be even fewer who have seen them.

At the entrance of the venue, there is an airplane set up, with alarming slogans on both sides: "We have five thousand years of history. Our ancestors have always been worthy of us!" "We have 400 million people. What good is it to have a lot of people?"

Most of the exhibited items in each section are displayed in the right half of the building. There are quite a few air defense charts, which are said to have been collected from the Air Defense School, Aviation School, Aviation Administration and other institutions. These are very necessary for our people who lack air defense knowledge, but unfortunately the characters are too small.

In addition to the various anti-poison products exhibited by the Civil Chemical Industry Society, several gas masks are also prepared in the venue for the audience to try on. There are photos and instructions on how to wear them, so you can wear them yourself without guidance. The reporter wore one and felt very uncomfortable. It is said that gas masks must be worn frequently at ordinary times, and you must take deep breaths when wearing them.

Now, our country can manufacture gas masks and rubber clothing and hats, and can manufacture them very well. Unfortunately, because purchasers are not enthusiastic, the cost cannot be reduced. A full set of anti-poison products costs thirty or forty yuan. This price is of course beyond the reach of the general public. Therefore, the association also has a display of anti-poison products for the public. This part tells the public several simple and emergency anti-poison methods, which are said to have considerable detoxification effects on poison gas.

Two Small Countries Participating in the World Games 215

— Junyi

In this year's World Games held in Berlin, there are two surprisingly small countries that officially participated. One is called Monaco and the other is called the Virgin Islands. Monaco is a small country in the south of France, with an area of only eight square miles and a population of only 22,000. It is the most famous casino in the world, and the government relies solely on gambling taxes to maintain it. As for the Virgin Islands, it is a small island in the Atlantic Ocean only seven nautical miles from New York, with an area of seventeen square miles and a population of 28,000. However, in winter, 70,000 to 80,000 foreigners come to escape the cold. There is also a special rule here: cars are not allowed to speed.

— Yachang

In the late Qing Dynasty, the revolution rose, and the wind rose from the clouds. Once, a foreigner said to Zhang Jingjiang: "When you are talking about revolution, it will be more powerful if you wear a red hat." Zhang smiled and said, "Of course! It's a pity that once you wear a red hat, you forget what you said." Zhang's words were very humorous, but he also saw through things. Times change people, and Yuan Shikai is an ironclad fact!

Snobbish Eyes 217

— Qiu Lang

Leaving aside the internal organs of the human body, the eyes in the head are the most important organs on the outside. Although the hands are also important, the eyes always assist when using the hands in actions. When using the eyes to see, there is no need for the hands to help them, so the eyes are the supreme treasure of the human body! Astrologers call them "double-suspended suns and moons," and even more praise the eyes of beautiful women as "autumn waves" and "autumn water." There are many good names, but although the eyes are precious, they are snobbish in nature! They only worship beauty, wealth, and power. They disdain to look at the poor and powerless. Therefore, it is popularly said that the eyes rot first when people die, or perhaps this is retribution.

Interesting Facts About Mosquitoes 218

— Yao Mingran

When it comes to dusk, mosquitoes fly everywhere as if they were in a general mobilization, and the buzzing sound is the only prelude. There are many records of this small flying insect by people of the past, but as in the "Collection of Poems from Suiyuan," the "Proclamation Against Mosquitoes" by a child says, "They come in groups, looking like bandits all over, drumming their wings and chanting loudly, with eyes full of the ghosts of essay examinations," which is borrowing the mosquito to scold people. Another example is "A Word for One Night," which compares mosquitoes to prostitutes, filling in the gaps in "Hearing the Oriole." The lyrics say, "Their name is cheap and their body is light, they love and hate when they encounter fire. Their small mouths are as sharp as blades, and they can sting people painfully. They can also heal people. Their charming voices wave the bewitching battle at night. They are so ruthless, stealing essence and sucking blood, yet they pretend to be hypocritical." It can be said that it is full of fun. In the past, Shan Shi of Qiantang Dou Shang wrote a poem about mosquitoes, "They risk their lives for blood, you are the most foolish in the world...", which can be used as a head-on school reunion drink for those who are greedy!

Youth and Old Age 222

— Chen Shaohua

Why do people grow old?

Why people grow old is truly a very interesting question, and also a question that concerns everyone personally. People only know that there is a difference between young and old due to age, but they do not know that it is actually due to the relationship of hormones in physiology. In our pre-pubescent stage, except for the reproductive parts, there is no difference between the sexes. Until the period of adolescent development, the function of internal secretion begins to flourish. All parts of the body are irrigated by hormones, and thus there is a distinction between male and female. As one grows older, the function of internal secretion gradually declines, and thus everything presents symbols of aging. Shanghai Shen Bao Supplement

Life 228

— Meng Hua

"Since you've been born, then live on, struggle on to live"! I see these words on everyone's face.

In the morning, when the thick fog hasn't dissipated, the street cleaner in the red uniform pushes the garbage truck towards Xī'ān Gate. There is a mountain of garbage there. On top of this garbage pile, there are dirty sows, greedily chewing on the moldy vegetable leaves, wagging their tiny tails. There are also dogs with drooping tails, crows and sparrows that fly down in a hurry and then fly away again, flies buzzing and chewing on the festering sores on the children's heads.

"Ding lang, ding lang--" The little bell hanging on the cart handle rings. The fog hasn't cleared yet, so you can't see any figures, only hear the particularly heavy sound of the bell in the fog. The children fly down from the pile of dirt, waiting and waiting.

As soon as the garbage is dumped, they concentrate on picking through it, their eyes fixed, grabbing with their hands, muttering in their mouths. Sometimes they also touch the sores on their heads and joints with dirty hands, where flies are holding a grand feast... Seen in the fog, they look like a group of ghosts, their voices as hoarse as those who have strained their vocal cords. What are they busy with? What are they doing it for?

The fathers of those children might be coolies, or rickshaw pullers, or workers, or maybe they don't have fathers at all. Who knows? But I believe that some of them are the sons of rickshaw pullers. During the hot summer days and cold winters, when the north wind is howling on the streets, swirling up gusts of dust, these fathers will curl up their bodies, open their mouths, and beg every passerby:

"Want a ride? I'll take you"!

Dust seeps into their mouths, sticking to their throats. But when another passerby comes along, they gaze at him with eager eyes, asking in a plaintive tone: "Sir, I'll take you"! At night, their voices are more like those of an old woman leading souls on the road. What are they busy with? What are they doing it for?

Maybe they also have young wives and young daughters. Maybe their wives and daughters, when the streetlights begin to shine brightly, dress up coquettishly and go to the market, using seductive eyes to tempt those single men. On the street, I see them. They always stand evasively in dark places, hiding in the shadows of the telephone poles, telling you in low voices: "Sir, have pity on me"!

Why do they stand in places without lights? Why are their voices so plaintive? Why do the hands they stretch out tremble? Why do they abandon their homes, leaving their relatives, their children, and running to this street in the dark night? I also remember winter nights. The night is so quiet and so cold. But in the corners of the alleys, there are often bursts of selling cries:

"Radishes as sweet as pears--spicy, come and trade!" "Sugar-coated cakes--cakes, oh cakes"!

Flight 229

— Cheng Xiuyang

Early in the morning, the old grandmother put on a sky-blue linen dress and went to the entrance of the village, leaning on her dragon-headed cane. She was so excited, as if her granddaughter had gone missing. She forgot the beads of sweat hanging from her forehead, she forgot the corns on her toes throbbing faintly, and like a young girl, she ran to the Five Mile Pavilion in one breath and sat down to rest.

In this town, the old grandmother is known as a woman with good fortune. In fact, because she is usually charitable and kind, and people in the town who have benefited from her just call her a woman with good fortune. Her only son died at the age of thirty, and within a year, his wife also passed away. An old grandmother, like a mother, had to raise the grandson and granddaughter left behind. Whenever she heard someone call her a woman with good fortune, she would always answer with red eyes: "Bad fate! I couldn't even raise a son until the end of his life"!

She finally raised a pair of siblings across "generations." Both of the children without parents listened to the old grandmother. When they were sent to school in the town, the old grandmother who was raising two generations became happy again like in her daughter-in-law days. Every night, under the kerosene lamp, she would put on her wide-rimmed old glasses and help the two children review their evening lessons. But when she often discovered that the primary school students had so many textbooks, she would sigh again:

"It's a different generation, it's really a different generation! There are so many lessons in foreign schools"?

Then she remembered a Three Character Classic when her son was studying. The teacher taught two sentences every day, but he still couldn't memorize them. Now the children have to read so many books, and those books are something she doesn't understand. She felt that the times were passing too quickly, but the children's liveliness and innocence were exactly like their father's, as if the times were forever stuck in her daughter-in-law days. She entrusted what she had hoped for in her son to the two children.

The children grew up as she had hoped. They went from elementary school to high school, and then to the city to study in middle school. But going to study in the city didn't satisfy her. She said she wasn't against going to foreign schools to study? But I have been raising the two children since they were young, and they can't leave me. They have to stay at school, and they have to do everything themselves, like making the bed and folding the quilt. Can the two children handle these things? The children's uncle came out to persuade her.

"Today's children are not like before. It's easy to make two round trips to the city every day. And now there is a holiday in school, and they can come home every six days. The children are very smart, and when they graduate from middle school in the future, they will be as prestigious as a scholar"!

Scholar, what a tempting name! This town has produced a total of two scholars, one of whom was her son. She agreed to let the siblings live and study in the city. She kept the scholar in her mouth: "Graduating from foreign school is a scholar, and my granddaughter will be a female scholar." She often woke up from dreams laughing.

But an incomprehensible "trend" took her female scholar away. This news caused a sensation in the whole town, and those who didn't care spoke coldly:

"What's the good of foreign schools? They specialize in making trouble, what is free love, isn't it just having affairs? It's really embarrassing for the town for a good family's daughter to do such a shameless thing"!

The old lady cried and shouted that she was suffering. She put on a blue linen dress like she was going crazy, and went to the foreign school in the city with her dragon-headed cane, wanting them to hand over her granddaughter. Finally, at the Five Mile Pavilion, she was dragged back by her neighbors. She didn't seem to be able to get over this, and rushed to her uncle's house, pointing at the uncle's forehead with her cane and scolding:

"Your sister died so miserably, and she left these two children, but you insisted on sending them to foreign school. You said, you said, you deceived me, an old woman, to be a scholar, and now people are gone. Give me back my granddaughter..."

She fell to the ground, hitting the stone bricks with her cane until she was exhausted. Many people persuaded her to go home.

The loss of the female scholar immediately affected the younger brother's education problem. The younger brother had already graduated from middle school, but the old grandmother who was raising two generations now refused to allow him to enter university no matter what. Going to university meant going to the provincial capital, and he would only come home twice a year during the winter and summer vacations. He had already caused trouble in the city, how could I control him if he went to the provincial capital? We only have this one child in our family! The old grandmother now rejected her grandson's request with righteous indignation.

That uncle still made the greatest effort to complete his nephew's studies. He endured countless venomous accusations from the old grandmother, and finally:

"...Girls will run away with other people, what will boys do? This town has never had a child who has gone to university before. This is not only your old lady's good fortune, but also the glory of this town! I want to compare it to the past again, it's simply like passing the imperial examination"! This is how he persuaded her.

The grandson came home twice every winter and summer vacation, and the old grandmother who was raising two generations still asked him about everything like he was in elementary school. When she saw so many thick foreign books, she put on her wide-rimmed old glasses to look at the lines of crab-like characters, and the name "foreign scholar" churned in her mind again. "That's right, what will boys do? Girls' hearts are outward-facing, it's always good to raise sons. A foreign scholar." Although she felt a slight sadness when she thought that her son had died too early. "I want to live a few more years, this grandson is whom I've raised since he was little, let me see him become a foreign scholar." She burned incense and prayed to her Guanyin Bodhisattva every day.

She was still so healthy. When she received the letter from her grandson saying that he had graduated from university and was coming home, she put on her sky-blue linen dress and ran to the Five Mile Pavilion in one breath. Whenever she met someone familiar coming towards her, she would answer that person's question, "My child graduated from university, he's become a foreign scholar!" She walked forward laughing.

The child came back, he was wearing foreign clothes, sitting in a rattan sedan as if he were the magistrate on patrol in the past, but in the rattan sedan behind him was a woman that this town had never seen before. The child told the old grandmother that she was his newly married granddaughter-in-law.

A bolt from the blue—what would boys do? Wasn't that just like having an affair? The same, the same, the down is dry and they want to fly outward, my life is bitter! When the old grandmother felt that all her hopes had been dashed, she thought of her son who died at the age of thirty, and cried loudly in front of his spirit tablet...

People Who Do Not Attend to Proper Business 230

— Fei Xiangdong

The people in the village all dislike Guo Desheng: this goes without saying because he does not attend to proper business. Regarding him, various discussions can be heard from time to time in teahouses and among gossiping village women. Some attribute Guo Desheng's downfall to his mother. This old woman has always doted on her son since he was little, and therefore always shielded him no matter what, refusing to discipline him properly. For example, once Guo Desheng harassed a woman on the road, and she loudly scolded him; but his mother, upon hearing this, came out to defend him, saying that the woman herself was indecent; why would Guo Desheng harass her and not someone else—she defended her son to everyone in this way—isn't this evidence that the woman is indecent? But everyone knew that Guo Desheng liked to do such vulgar things, so they responded with cold laughter. Thus, his

Page 20

mother had no choice but to quickly arrange a marriage for her son: Guo Desheng is now a married man. Some people thought that Guo Desheng was born bad; in the future, he might even do worse things. In the village, people who valued themselves even slightly avoided him; they did not associate with him. Guo Desheng's friends, needless to say, were only opium smokers or gamblers.

Gambler Fang Aqiang was a very close friend of Guo Desheng. He began to take Guo Desheng to gambling dens, enticing him to gamble. Seeing gambling there as a good way to get rich, he completely immersed himself in it. He lost all the money he and his mother had; he was very frustrated. Fang Aqiang, however, said to him, "Your gambling method is wrong; you need more capital to succeed." Hearing these words, Guo Desheng thought in his heart that this might be true; and since he had to win back the money he had lost, he returned to his home, where he had not been for three days.

Guo Desheng's wife was a virtuous woman; at home, she fulfilled her responsibilities as a daughter-in-law. However, her husband's neglect of proper business made her very sad. She did her best to persuade him to change his current absurd life, but to no avail. This evening, Guo Desheng returned. At first, he was much gentler than before, asking her for money; but when she asked what he needed it for, he could not answer. Moreover, she really had no money. Gradually, Guo Desheng became impatient, and he insisted on getting it; even her jewelry would do. She refused, resisting his forceful robbery. As a result, she was pushed to the floor. Raising his head, her husband revealed a fierce face, pointing at her and scolding, "You vile woman! If you don't listen to me, I'll kick you to death!" The woman began to sob, which made him even more unbearable. Raising his foot, he kicked her back. She fell down again. Then, disregarding everything, he snatched her keys, opened the cabinet, and took all the jewelry she had brought with her when she married and exchanged it for gambling money. He then went to find Fang Aqiang and returned to that place.

This time, I must win back what I lost, Guo Desheng thought in his heart. He stayed there until the next morning. Unexpectedly, he lost everything again.

Fang Aqiang truly deserved to be called an old gambler. Seeing Guo Desheng looking dejected, he walked over, patted him on the shoulder, and said, "What's wrong? You look like a defeated soldier! Desheng, winning and losing are common occurrences for soldiers. You mustn't lose heart! Go get some more money and try again. If luck comes your way, it will be incredible!" Guo Desheng turned his face and gave him a smile, but how bitter that smile was.

Gradually, Guo Desheng became a well-known gambler in the village. The fate of the virtuous daughter-in-law had reached its darkest point. She began to fall silent, not responding to him and no longer trying to persuade him with earnest words. Everything in the house had been secretly pawned off by Guo Desheng; even his doting mother shed tears at this. Before long, the old mother, unable to bear the worries caused by her son's neglect of proper business, quietly passed away one night in a drizzling autumn rain, without even a groan, abandoning her son and daughter-in-law. At the moment of her death, she spoke in a repentant tone, saying intermittently, "I was wrong!... My whole life was wrong!... Desheng, if you don't repent, I really... Desheng, you must properly... properly advise your husband who neglects proper business!" The young daughter-in-law only shook her head, her eyes filled with tears, watching her mother-in-law close her eyes, forever ceasing the beating of her heart. At this time, Guo Desheng also occasionally thought about repenting, and he did not go to the gambling den for two days. However, he was a notorious bad guy, and who would give him a chance to reform? So, when the gambler Fang Aqiang appeared before him again, he took the only winter cotton robe he had left and went out again.

Seeing that her husband would never turn back, and that the house was completely empty, the young daughter-in-law felt that everything was empty and hopeless. On a night when Guo Desheng did not return, she hanged herself. This tragedy caused Guo Desheng to be despised and cursed by the villagers; until one day, this person who did not attend to proper business suddenly disappeared. Where he went, even Fang Aqiang did not know. "Let such a person disappear from our village forever," people said. Indeed, Guo Desheng never returned; now, his dilapidated house has collapsed.

Remnant Sounds

Traffic Department Shanghai Radio Station (Call Sign XQHC Weekly Rate 1300)

In view of the importance of women's education, in order to enable women to increase practical knowledge in entertainment, it is now scheduled from July 13 (Monday), every Monday afternoon from 5:15 to 5:30, Miss Hu Shen will be specially invited to host the women's program. All practical knowledge of women's daily life and general knowledge will be broadcast as much as possible, so that women in general families can acquire living knowledge above the standard, so as to achieve the practical benefits of broadcast education, and to change the decadent life of women who only know how to play mahjong and listen to low-level broadcasts. In order to facilitate the inquiry of women, the station has specially created an item of "Women's Correspondence" from now on, and welcomes women from this and other ports to directly send letters of inquiry. The rules of this item are as follows: All listeners are welcome to send letters of inquiry about various practical problems related to women and the daily housework life of women: Each letter is limited to three questions: The correspondence must be attached with sufficient return postage stamps; If the correspondence is general, it should be broadcast in the air, so that the majority of women can get appropriate guidance at the same time; If listeners raise various practical problems of women in their letters, and it is worthy of public discussion, they will be carefully studied in the air to achieve the benefit of mutual encouragement; Correspondence should be sent to the "Women's Correspondence Office", No. 137 Sassoon Building, Shanghai Traffic Department Radio Station, and do not write personal names.

Since the prevalence of self-broadcasting in Shanghai, opera groups have sprung up like bamboo shoots after a rain, and they have become increasingly numerous. However, they are isolated and have no contact with each other. It is always difficult to deal with affairs with one heart and one mind. Recently, various groups such as Datong, Furong, Shanghai, and Yifeng have organized a sound "Shanghai Dance and Drama Association" in order to facilitate the study of the progress of dance art and to discuss the development of business. It is also heard that a joint symposium of all opera groups in Shanghai will be held at the National Primary School at 9 am on the 12th of this month to jointly discuss all the steps of preparing for the organization. It is expected that there will be a new atmosphere in the dance in the future.

Mr. Liu Xinkai, an expert in Chinese studies, was hired by Tian Xiaode Medicine, Li Da Wang, Daoxiangcun Zheng Da Wang, and Mao Shi Optical Company to give lectures on the states at the Guohua Radio Station. From July 1st, from 3:00 to 3:40 pm, please pay attention to all walks of life.

Anniversary of Two Artists' Death 236

Qingjian composer Nie Er drowned in Japan, and the 18th of this month is the anniversary of his death. Over the past year. The oppression of the enemy has become more and more serious, and the roars of people who are unwilling to be slaves have also increased in direct proportion. In this upsurge of popular movement, progressive songs are very popular among the people. In every mass gathering, those abundant songs are repeatedly sung by the masses, and Mr. Nie Er's songs such as "Graduation Song" are even more welcomed by the masses.

In order to commemorate this great composer, the city's Songwriters Association, Chinese Poetry Society, Roaring Singing Troupe, Roaring Singing Troupe, Amateur Singing Team, New Voice Choir, Ant Society Singing Society, Public Education Hall Singing Troupe, Minzhi Middle School Singing Class, Mass Singing Society, Time Singing Troupe, Pingliang Road Singing Troupe, Hualong Road Singing Troupe, Eight Immortals Bridge Mass Singing Society, and Liangcai Singing Society have jointly launched a commemorative conference on the anniversary of his death. In addition to reporting on Nie Er's life and singing all his works, it is fair to prepare to sing the patriotic songs made by others in front of his grave. "Because various items are in progress and need to be prepared urgently," they borrowed Minzhi Middle School to hold the first preparatory meeting at 7:30 pm yesterday. We will report on the results of the meeting later.

The anniversary of Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu's death has already arrived. August 2nd (July 16th in the lunar calendar) is an unforgettable tragic anniversary for the colleagues of the Star Company and even the Chinese film audience. The Star colleagues will all go to the Pure Land Nunnery, the place where Mr. Zhengqiu's coffin is placed, to hold a solemn anniversary sacrifice. As for the issue of Mr. Zheng's burial, it is being discussed by Mr. Zhengqiu's family and the Chaozhou Fellow Association.

George Ge's "My Diary" 237

China's first masterpiece of child stars, "My Diary," has been published. The content describes all kinds of anecdotes during the filming of "The Lost Lamb" in Suzhou, especially about Cai Chusheng and Chen Juanjuan. There are also many copperplate prints. Each issue only sells for 1.2 cents of national currency. Postage stamps are commonly used for correspondence purchases. Qianqiu Publishing House, No. 4, Lane 153, South of Kad Road Post Office, Shanghai, publishes it.

Introducing the Famous Literary Work "The Adventures of Pinocchio in Africa" 238

The illustrated novel "The Adventures of Pinocchio in Africa" is one of the world's famous works of juvenile literature and is comparable to "The Adventures of Pinocchio". The content describes a wooden puppet's adventure into Africa to explore the wonders, experiencing various dangerous, strange and interesting encounters, from not knowing how to do it to becoming an emperor, from an emperor to a slave, and finally escaping this dark Africa. Therefore, it is tortuous, humorous, and of great educational value. The original author is Italy's Xue Lübini, and it is said that it has now been translated into Chinese by Jiang Manru (and has been revised by Mr. Wang Tianran). The translation is unusually prosperous and lively. Children and adults should read it, and there are eighteen illustrations in the book, which add a lot of interest. The entire book is more than two hundred pages thick and is finely printed in regular script. The actual price of each book is only 70 cents. The Reading World Bookstore at 314 Jinshenfu Road publishes it, and the Life Bookstore and Shanghai Magazine Company also sell it.
